Suggested wording for capability meeting with underperforming staff When speaking with the employee, frame this as an opportunity for growth rather than punishment. Emphasize that the company wants them to succeed and that the process is designed to give them clear benchmarks and resources. Avoid accusatory language — use “we’ve noticed” instead of “you’ve failed.” Offer a structured timeline, review points, and a path to resolution. Tone matters as much as content here.
